  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_41bbf76b-84e4-41dc-a05d-a229f4db3062'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

  <span id="freeText17264013262621022400" style="display:none">The third installment in the all-new series from the #1 NEW YORK TIMES bestselling author Maggie Stiefvater!<br /><br />Blue Sargent has found things. For the first time in her life, she has friends she can trust, a group to which she can belong. The Raven Boys have taken her in as one of their own. Their problems have become hers, and her problems have become theirs. <br /><br />The trick with found things, though, is how easily they can be lost.<br /><br />Friends can betray.<br />Mothers can disappear.<br />Visions can mislead.<br />Certainties can unravel.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17264013262621022400" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/17973865-pear001"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1373056057i/17973865._UY100_CR16,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/17973865-pear001">Pear001</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">1) I love this series. My favorite by far and I would always give it a ten but let's pretend I'm not being biased and 9.9/10?<br/>2) there are four boys an<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">1) I love this series. My favorite by far and I would always give it a ten but let's pretend I'm not being biased and 9.9/10?<br />2) there are four boys and one girl. One boy had a brief crush on her and one who may be in love with her and she with him. There is also one boy with a HEAVILY implied crush on another boy. Romance is not as strong as you'd think it would be considering genre and the whole "kiss your true love and he dies" thing but when it does creep up its swoon worthy.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

      $('span_class_gr-hyperlink_sort_order_span_tip_559').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>    </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/764866058" />
    <a title="Zemira (Kylo Ren fangirl) Warner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4995937-zemira-kylo-ren-fangirl-warner"><img alt="Zemira (Kylo Ren fangirl) Warner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1512674314p2/4995937.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/764866058?book_show_action=true">Nov 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zemira (Kylo Ren fangirl) Warner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zemira (Kylo Ren fangirl) Warner" href="/user/show/4995937-zemira-kylo-ren-fangirl-warner">Zemira (Kylo Ren fangirl) Warner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">people with good taste</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4995937-zemira-kylo-ren-fangirl-warner?shelf=won">won</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4995937-zemira-kylo-ren-fangirl-warner?shelf=boarding-school">boarding-school</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4995937-zemira-kylo-ren-fangirl-warner?shelf=hot-guys">hot-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4995937-zemira-kylo-ren-fangirl-warner?shelf=i-own">i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4995937-zemira-kylo-ren-fangirl-warner?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4995937-zemira-kylo-ren-fangirl-warner?shelf=ghosts">ghosts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4995937-zemira-kylo-ren-fangirl-warner?shelf=i-want-to-write-like-this">i-want-to-write-like-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4995937-zemira-kylo-ren-fangirl-warner?shelf=best-of-2014">best-of-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4995937-zemira-kylo-ren-fangirl-warner?shelf=magical-realism">magical-realism</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer764866058" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9273754683184407305"><b>I only need one thing----> Ronan x Adam. </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384460700ra/6880409.gif' width='330' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384460700ra/6880410.gif' width='330' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The story picks up where it left off. Boys are starting school again and Blue's mother is still missing. They're still trying to find Glendower, the long lost king. Gray Man's employed is in Henrietta looking for a payback. Now, I don't want to reveal anything else about the plot cause even the blurb is rather vague. <br/><br/>What I want to talk about are the characters. It seems Adam is the main one this time. Others all had their chapters but I feel as if he was</span>
  <span id="freeText9273754683184407305" style="display:none"><b>I only need one thing----&gt; Ronan x Adam. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384460700ra/6880409.gif" width="330" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384460700ra/6880410.gif" width="330" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story picks up where it left off. Boys are starting school again and Blue's mother is still missing. They're still trying to find Glendower, the long lost king. Gray Man's employed is in Henrietta looking for a payback. Now, I don't want to reveal anything else about the plot cause even the blurb is rather vague. <br><br>What I want to talk about are the characters. It seems Adam is the main one this time. Others all had their chapters but I feel as if he was in all of them a lot more. He's my favorite Raven Boy, like I mentioned a hundred times already. He's still hardworking as ever. Honorable, honest and proud. He's also spending more time with Ronan, if you know what I mean. *wink, wink* <br><br>Then there's Ronan. *sigh* This guy! I mean, he's like a feral cat you want to bring home but you're scared it's going to ruin your sofa. You never know what to expect from him. He's unpredictable, wild, but at the same time extremely loyal to his family and friends. There is still so much we don't know about him. <br><br>Gansey is still a mystery to me. At times I think he has no personality and he's just there in every chapter. I know he's suppose to be the King of the gang but I don't see it. :/ Everybody likes him-boys in school, new people he meets and even Adam let go of his jealousy. He's helpful in a way a human can help a paranormal creature-basically not. I guess I'm the only one who doesn't care about his character. <br><br>Blue's trying to find her missing mother and is dealing with her feelings towards Gansey at the same time. She was focused and determined throughout the whole book. She might even discover some hidden power deep inside her. <br><br>If you're expecting kisses in this book, like me, you'll just going to have to wait for the 4th installment. Even though the book was focused towards the character development, romance was pushed even further out back. There were some progress and Pynch shippers will be happy to hear it. I can't wait for the next book because I feel that's when Pynch is going to happen. <br><br>The pacing was perfect and every chapter ended on a cliffhanger which made me scream. The book was unputdownable. And the writing is poetic. At times I had to go back and re-read parts because I thought there was something between the lines. How Maggie does this every time, I don't know. She'll always be on my auto-buy list. <br><br>Cover is beautiful. I love the colors but I'm not sure who's on it. Blue? It could be her. <br><br><a href="http://yafanatic.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397119801i/9233870.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_2177688308" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2177688308" />
    <a title="Miranda Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/71848701-miranda-reads"><img alt="Miranda Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1592243041p2/71848701.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2177688308?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miranda Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miranda Reads" href="/user/show/71848701-miranda-reads">Miranda Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71848701-miranda-reads?shelf=ya-series">ya-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71848701-miranda-reads?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2177688308" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15988899343178922878"><blockquote>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1537882690i/26352851._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><b>Faith in <s>humanity</s> Young Adult Lit restored</b> <blockquote>
  <i>“Blue,” he warned, but his voice was chaotic. This close, his throat was scented with mint and wool sweater and vinyl car seat, and Gansey, just Gansey.<br/><br/>She said, “I just want to pretend. I want to pretend that I could.” </i>
</blockquote> I would normally poke fun at YA for the <b> drama and the weird boy-smells</b> but I honestly can't. <br/><br/>Maggie Stiefvater has done such a wonderful job building this story that there's no room to be a <b>sarcastic little snit </b>about it. <br/><br/><b>
  <u>It</u></b></span>
  <span id="freeText15988899343178922878" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1537882690i/26352851._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><b>Faith in <s>humanity</s> Young Adult Lit restored</b> <blockquote>
  <i>“Blue,” he warned, but his voice was chaotic. This close, his throat was scented with mint and wool sweater and vinyl car seat, and Gansey, just Gansey.<br><br>She said, “I just want to pretend. I want to pretend that I could.” </i>
</blockquote> I would normally poke fun at YA for the <b> drama and the weird boy-smells</b> but I honestly can't. <br><br>Maggie Stiefvater has done such a wonderful job building this story that there's no room to be a <b>sarcastic little snit </b>about it. <br><br><b>
  <u>It would be sacrilege. </u>
</b><br><br>Blue, Gansey, Ronan, Adam and Noah are about to go on one hellofa journey.<br><br><b> People will die, </b>relationships will be broken and throughout all of that<b> they have each other</b> to lean on. Maggie Stiefvater creates such well-fleshed out characters that <b>I sometimes forget they aren't real. </b><br><br>The rapport between the five of them just ties this entire story together. <blockquote>
  <i> “What do we do now?" Gansey asked.<br><br>From the other room, Calla bellowed, "GO BUY US PIZZA. WITH EXTRA CHEESE, RICHIE RICH."<br><br>Blue said, "I think she's starting to like you.” </i>
</blockquote> Gah! I just want them all to be real. <blockquote>
<i>Adam was beginning to realize that he hadn't known Ronan at all. Or rather, he had known part of him and assumed it was all of him.</i><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1519191363i/25096331._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote>You know that feeling when you want to just pull a character from the pages? Me too. <br><br><b> I'm so unconditionally in love with this series.</b> <br><br><b>Audiobook Comments</b><br>Will Patton is a mastermind. With 5 rotating main characters, he manages to give each one a distinct voice and each voice has a life of its own. It's gotten to the point that when I read this book, instead of my internal monologue voice, I "hear" his voice. This man is probably my favorite reader ever.<br><br>Credit for the fantastic Ronan art:<a href="https://xla-hainex.deviantart.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">xla-hainex</a> <br><br><a href="http://bit.ly/33ii2CT" rel="nofollow noopener">YouTube</a> | <a href="http://www.mirandareads.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/miranda.reads/?hl=en" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/Miranda_Reads" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | Snapchat @miranda.reads <br><br>Happy Reading!</span>

<div id="review_2188933282" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2188933282" />
    <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale"><img alt="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577855357p2/69106439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2188933282?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale">Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780545424974" href="/book/show/24612656-blue-lily-lily-blue">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2188933282" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10655796388769971836"><i>“Humans were so circular; they lived the same slow cycles of joy and misery over and over, never learning. Every lesson in the universe had to be taught billions of times, and it never stuck.”</i><br/><br/>Oh my!!! She did it once again!<br/>Whenever I’m convinced that Maggie’s last book was already the peak of perfection she always manages to persuade me otherwise! I don’t really know how she does it, but she’s soo damn good at what she does that it’s almost impossible not to love her books!!! <3 <br/>Needless to say </span>
  <span id="freeText10655796388769971836" style="display:none"><i>“Humans were so circular; they lived the same slow cycles of joy and misery over and over, never learning. Every lesson in the universe had to be taught billions of times, and it never stuck.”</i><br><br>Oh my!!! She did it once again!<br>Whenever I’m convinced that Maggie’s last book was already the peak of perfection she always manages to persuade me otherwise! I don’t really know how she does it, but she’s soo damn good at what she does that it’s almost impossible not to love her books!!! &lt;3 <br>Needless to say that it was exactly the same with <b>“Blue Lily, Lily Blue”</b>!! XD<br><br>This book was so marvellous!!<br>I loved “The Raven Boys”,<br>I adored “The Dream Thieves” <br>BUT I was a complete sucker for “Blue Lily, Lily Blue”!!!<br>If it wasn’t already official, it definitely is now! I’m Maggie Stiefvater trash through and through and I just can’t imagine a world without her books anymore!!! *lol*<br><br>They give me <b>LIFE!!!</b> They make me feel! And over those last three months they’ve actually become the air that I breathe!! <br>I’m <u>IN LOVE</u> with Maggie’s writing <b>AND</b> each and every single one of her Raven Boys! &lt;333<br>Their struggles, their anger, their pain, their hopes, their fears, their dreams, their vulnerability!!! It all feels so damn real!!! GOSH!!! I can’t even!!! XD<br>With every single book they’ve become even more palpable and real! I feel so strongly for those four boys it’s like they are actual people, like they are some of my closest friends! =))<br>And for that I’ll always be grateful!!! Maggie you’re an amazing writer!!! I hope you know that!! ;-P<br>(Just in case no one ever bothered to tell you… Which I truly doubt, but still!! *lol*)<br><br><b>The plot:</b><br><br><i>”The most infuriating part about Maura’s disappearance was that Blue didn’t know if she was supposed to be consumed by worry or anger. She vacillated wildly between the two, occasionally burning herself out and feeling nothing at all.”</i><br><br>As the title of the book already indicates Blue is the focus of the third book! This time around we’re dealing with the troubles of 300 Fox Way and the huge void that was left after Maura’s sudden and completely unexpected disappearance at the end of book two. Of course this wouldn’t be a Maggie Stiefvater book if we wouldn’t get plenty of additional information about the lives of the Raven Boys as well. So don’t worry and be assured that there will be many moments with our lovely and awesome boys. I guess I don’t even need to mention it, but I’m certain you’ll appreciate each and every single one of them! ;-) <br><br><b>The characters:</b><br><br><i>”Blue was perfectly aware that it was possible to have a friendship that wasn’t all-encompassing, that wasn’t blinding, deafening, maddening, quickening. It was just that now that she’d had this kind, she didn’t want the other.”</i><br><br><u>
  <b>This is the moment I make sure to warn you about upcoming spoilers and quotes! ;-) If you haven’t read the book already you better click that tiny “x” button! It’s sound advice, I swear! ;-P </b>
</u><br><br><b>Gansey – The Knight:</b><br><br><i>”The Camaro was like Gansey tonight: terrifying and thrilling, willing to do whatever she asked.”</i><br><br>I swear, this time around I almost couldn’t bear it to read Gansey’s POV!!! My heart is bleeding for this poor boy and the more I get to know him the more it hurts!!! He’s such a gentle, honourable and delicate soul! If I had to draw a comparison I’d say the Gansey in “Blue Lily, Lily Blue” was like a Chinese Ming Vase: So damn beautiful to look at but so fragile and ancient that you could literally see the fissures spreading in his armour! He is so broken on the inside and I think Blue’s conversation with Malory made that more than just clear. When he told her that Gansey didn’t just claw his face but also was completely traumatized after his incident with the hornets I actually felt a lump in my throat!! This chapter was so intense I almost forgot to breathe and even though it hurts me so much to watch Gansey, I still want to know how it all ends!!! Please Maggie, don’t let him die!!! &gt;_&lt;<br><br><i>”There was another pause, and Gansey realized she’d hung up. He leaned back against the fridge, eyes closed, guilty, comforted, wild, contained. In twenty-four hours, he’d be waiting for this again.</i><br><br><i>”Gansey didn’t so much visit as get absorbed.<br>He loved it. He wanted to be a part of this world, even though he understood there were endless reasons why he could never be. Blue was the natural result of a home like this: confident, strange, credulous, curious. And here he was: neurotic, rarified, the product of something else entirely.”</i><br><br><i>”It’s very decent of you,” he continued, “to not say anything about it to me. It’s more than I deserved. But know that I’ve regretted it, a lot.”</i><br><br><b>Blue – The Mirror:</b><br><br><i>”Maura was always telling her, Look at the potential you hold inside yourself!<br>Potential for other people, though. Not for Blue.</i><br><br>Since this book was rather Blue centred I finally had the feeling that I actually got to know her a little bit better! No matter what I did, I just couldn’t seem to be able to grasp her character in the first two books. But now that I read “Blue Lily, Lily Blue” it was so much easier to understand her motives and the reasons why she’s acting the way she does. I felt so sorry for her because she actually suffered a lot! &gt;_&lt; The situation with her missing mother, her relationship to the boys and her intense feelings for Gansey, the troubles of finding a good college and last but not least Persephone’s unexpected death!!! T_T It’s quite a lot to have on your plate when you’re as young as her and I think she was very brave and strong for keeping it together for so long! &lt;3<br><br><i>”She was tired of Persephone and Calla and her mother withholding information because Blue wasn’t psychic. Of not being able to daydream of fancy colleges because she wasn’t rich. Of not being able to hold Gansey’s hand because they couldn’t hurt Adam’s feelings and not being able to kiss Gansey’s mouth because she didn’t want to kill him. She was tired of knowing that he was going to die and being afraid that her mother would, too.</i><br><br><b>Adam – The Magician:</b><br><br><i>”He knew he was different since aligning himself more tightly with the ley line this summer. He was himself, but more powerful. Himself, but less human.”</i><br><br>I think I am in love with Adam Parrish! Like seriously, completely and utterly in love!!! &lt;333 This boy is soo damn freaking <b>A.M.A.Z.I.N.G</b> and the Ronan in me just can’t stop to love him!!! XD Adam has become everything I wished him to be!!! He’s so strong now and his powers are growing with each and every single day!!! And it’s not just his powers, it’s the person he’s becoming!! Yes, some of his actions might be considered to be on the dark side, but oh damn this only makes him even more intriguing!!! &lt;333 His sharp mind constantly caused me to swoon and his thoughts… OH GOD, his philosophical thoughts were just epic!!! XD I loved that he was the only one who was smart enough to realise that Gansey is on the list and I was so happy that he finally managed to jump over his own shadow and accepted help!!! And the conversation with his father!??!! ARGH!!! It made me so damn angry!!! I hate and despise this man with a fierce passion and I really hope I will never read anything about him again!!! *growls*<br><br><i>”The students kept coming in. Adam kept watching. He was good at this part, the observing of others. It was himself that he couldn’t seem to study or understand. How he despised them, how he wanted to be them. How pointless to summer in Maine, how much he wanted to do it. How affected he found their speech, how he coveted their lazy monotones. He couldn’t tell how all of these things could be equally true.”</i><br><br><i>”What an impossible and miraculous and hideous thing this was. An ugly plan hatched by an ugly boy now dreamt into ugly life. From dream to reality. How appropriate it was that Ronan, left to his own devices, manifested beautiful cars and beautiful birds and tenderhearted brothers, while Adam, when given the power, manifested a filthy string of perverse murders.</i><br><br><i>”Adam was quiet as he weighted the options. His face was strange and delicate in the sharp light of Gansey’s head beam. Swiftly, and without explanation, he reached out to touch the cavern wall. Although he was not a dream thing, he was now one of Cabeswater’s things, and it was hard not to see it in the way his fingers spidered across the wall and in the blackness of his eyes as they gazed at nothing.</i><br><br><b>Ronan – The Greywaren:</b><br><br><i>”Ronan was always saying that he never lied, but he wore a liar’s face.”</i><br><br>Another thing that’s become official with this book is the simple fact that Ronan and I must be twins!!! I swear, Ronan is so damn relatable and I just love him for it! XD Deep down within him he has such a tender and lovely heart and I know if he’d read this, he’d probably kill me for saying it out loud! *LOL* It’s still true, Ronan!!! DUH!! ;-P Well, anyway! I really enjoyed seeing that he finally opened up to his friends and there were so many beautiful and affectionate moments that my heart literally combusted whenever I read about him. I know some of my friends got slightly annoyed by the many Ronan updates *cough* Maks *cough* but I just couldn’t help it!!! XD I was really surprised when he took Adam to the Barns and actually admitted that Matthew is one of his dreams and it broke my heart to find out how lonely he truly is. <i>“Lonesome.”</i> it was the word that dominated Adam’s thoughts and I really hope that he won’t be alone anymore!!! &lt;333<br>To sum it all up: RONAN IS PRECIOUS AF!! *lol* ;-P<br><br><i>The smile widened and sharpened yet more. “It’s not your problem, Gansey.”<br>He was so much more dangerous when he wasn’t angry. And he was right: Gansey didn’t want to know.</i><br><br><i>”As always, Adam was reminded of how Ronan belonged in this place. Something about the familiar way he stood as he searched for ripe fruit implied that he had done it many times before. It made it easy to understand that Ronan had grown up here and would grow old here. Easy to see how to exile him was to excise his soul.</i><br><br><i>Ronan scoffed. Him, fear for his own life. But there was something in his eyes, still. He studied his hands and admitted, “I’ve dreamt him a box of EpiPens. I dream cures for stings all the time. I carry one. I put them in the Pig. I have them all over Monmouth.”</i><br><br><b>Noah – The Ghost:</b><br><br><i>”Noah sat in the middle of the floor, papers all around him, a mint plant spilling dirt by his hand. He was all hunched over and shadowless, his form slight and streaky, barely visible at all. He was crying again. <br>In a very small voice, he told Blue, “You said I could use your energy.”</i><br><br>Noah Czerny is so adorable! That boy has such a wonderful character and it makes me so damn sad that he’s a ghost and dead! I love his cheerful and bouncy nature and I adore how tender and caring he is with the others! Unfortunately there is also a lot of anger and sadness in him and I’m not ashamed to admit that I actually sobbed when he had his breakdown at Monmouth. T_T I just want my baby to be happy, but I can’t see a future for him and it breaks my freaking heart to know that his story most certainly won’t have a happy ending! *weeps*<br><br><i>”Noah reappeared. He plucked four and a half oak leaves out of Blue’s spiky hair and blew some leaf crumbs from the bridge of Adam’s nose.”</i><br><br><b>Mr. Gray:</b><br><br><i>” ’A cowards’s heart is no prize, but the man of valor deserves a shining helmet.’ “</i><br><br>I love Mr. Gray!!! His conversations with Blue were so sweet and honest and I really liked how their relationship developed throughout the entire book! &lt;3 Mr. Gray was the perfect father figure and I wonder what will happen in the last book! I mean Artemus finally returned so I guess this will cause quite some trouble between him and Maura. Uh oh! &gt;_&lt;<br><br><i>”In my experience,” the Gray Man said, “the badasses are the most scared. I just avoid being inappropriately frightened.”</i><br><br><b>The Greenmantle’s:</b><br><br><i>Afterward, Piper said, “If we had a puppy, it could pick up those beans for us.”<br>Greenmantle had replied, “And then we could sacrifice it and use its blood to activate the doll.”<br>“Will you marry me?” she asked.</i><br><br>Whilst I can’t deny that the Greenmantle’s were pretty entertaining I still want to use this space to point out that they were completely crazy!! *lol* I mean Mr. Gray threatened Piper and they were as cool as if they’d only talk about the weather! They were always so composed and nonchalant and this kind of made them creepy! XD I guess the word I’m searching for is “psychopath”! Yep, that’s it! They were both psychopaths! And truth be told, Piper might have even been the bigger one! *lol*<br><br><b>The friendships:</b><br><br><u>
  <b>Ronan &amp; Blue:</b>
</u><br><br><i>”Ronan looked at Blue, eyes narrowed. She didn’t look away. <br>This was a game she sometimes played with Ronan Lynch: Who would look away first?<br>It was always a draw.”</i><br><br>Aww! Those two! <u>THOSE TWO!</u> I loved how Ronan consoled Blue when she saw her mother in the lake and the fact he handed her the ghost light even though he knew that he would be alone and in the dark!!! OMG! I think this was one of the most precious moments of the entire book and my heart filled with so much warmth when I read it! &lt;3 I really like that they are finally beginning to trust each other and I can’t wait to see more of their friendship! <br><br><i>”It was amazing that she and Ronan didn’t get along better, because they were different brands of the same impossible stuff.”</i><br><br><i>”For a moment they remained that way, Ronan holding her as tightly as he would hold his brother Matthew, his cheek on her shoulder.”</i><br><br><u>
  <b>Gansey &amp; Adam:</b>
</u><br><br><i>”His noble and oblivious and optimistic friend was slowly opening his eyes and seeing the world for what it was, and it was filthy, and violent, and profane, and unfair. Adam had always thought that was what he wanted – for Gansey to know. But now he wasn’t sure. Gansey wasn’t like anyone else, and suddenly Adam wasn’t sure that he really wanted him to be.”</i><br><br>I was so damn happy that Gansey and Adam actually managed to overcome their troubles! It was awesome to see that their friendship didn’t only survive their problems but also got even stronger than before! The moment when Gansey and Ronan showed up at court immediately caused me to grin like crazy and their gesture made me so happy I almost burst with joy! I loved that they supported him so much and I really don’t want those boys to ever argue again! I’m so glad that Adam finally realised that Gansey is only trying to be his friend!!! &lt;333<br><br><i>”Adam couldn’t remember how they had managed to fight so continuously over the summer. Gansey, his best friend, his stupid and kind and marvelous best friend.”</i><br><br><i>”Now he could see that it wasn’t charity Gansey was offering. It was just truth. And something else: friendship of the unshakable kind. Friendship you could swear on. That could be busted nearly to breaking and come back stronger than before.”</i><br><br><u>
  <b>Gansey &amp; Noah:</b>
</u><br><br><i>”Don’t be afraid,” Noah said unexpectedly. Reaching out, he pulled Gansey’s hand away from his ear. Gansey hadn’t even realized that he was still touching it softly. Leaning forward, Noah blew his cool, corpse breath over Gansey’s ear. “Nothing there. You’re just tired.”<br>Gansey shivered a little.”</i><br><br>I absolutely adore the relationship of those two boys! They are both gentle souls that try their best to deal with their pain and they seem to understand each other in a way no one else does. Noah knows all of Gansey’s secrets, but he’d never judge him or tell the others. They trust each other completely and even though Noah is a ghost, Gansey always treats him like a normal person! &lt;3 It’s obvious that Noah cares about Gansey and his tender gestures only seem to emphasise his feelings! XD<br><br><i>There was nothing inherently guilty about the moment except that Gansey burned with guilt and thrill and desire and the nebulous feeling of being truly known. It was on the inside of him, and the inside was all Noah ever really paid attention to. <br>The other boy wore a knowing expression.<br>”Don’t tell the others,” Gansey said.<br>“I’m dead,” Noah replied. “Not stupid.”</i><br><br><b>The ships:</b><br><br><b>
  <u>Gansey &amp; Blue:</u>
</b><br><br><i>”Casually, out of view of Ronan, making sure Adam was still sleeping, Gansey dangled his hand between the driver’s seat and the door. Palm up, fingers stretched back to Blue.”</i><br><br>Their desperate attempts to keep away from each other literally killed me and their nightly phone calls tugged at my heartstrings! There were so many sweet moments between those two but they both know that it can’t end well and it’s hurting them so much that they can’t even seem to be able to breathe whenever they are in each other’s company! <b>JEEZ LOUISE!!!</b> Their love is so bittersweet it’s tearing me apart!!! &lt;3 <br><br><i>It was so strange to see him without his Richard Campbell Gansey III guise on in public that Blue couldn’t stop staring at his face. No – it wasn’t his face. It was the way he stood, his shoulders shrugged, chin ducked, gaze from below uncertain eyebrows.<br>“SHE WAS ALL RIGHT,” Jesse assured him.<br>“My head knew that,” Gansey said. “But the rest of me didn’t.”</i><br><br><i>”And then we never speak of it again,” Gansey said, mocking himself softly, and Blue was so glad of it, because she had played the words from that night over and over in her mind and wanted to know he had, too.”</i><br><br><b>
  <u>Ronan &amp; Adam aka Ronam:</u>
</b><br><br><i>”Maybe I dreamt you,” he said.<br>“Thanks for the straight teeth, then,” Adam replied.</i><br><br><b>RONAN FREAKIN LYNCH COURTED ADAM PARRISH!!!</b> &lt;333 OMG!!! I will never get over this!! I mean Ronan dreamed him a lotion for his hands!! He placed a cassette in his car and named it: “PARRISH’S HONDAYOTA ALONE TIME“ AND it seems like he actually paid him nightly visits in his apartment!!! IN ADAM’S FREAKIN APARTMENT!!! ADFSJKLMNÖ!!! Oh my!!! I’m combusting! &lt;333 There were so many awesome Ronam moments in this book and I can’t even explain how happy they made me! *lol* I loved how smug Ronan was about Adam being the magician and my heart melted when he tried to console him when Persephone died!!! Oh and when they blackmailed Greenmantle!? So, so perfect, so epic!!! They are such an awesome TEAM!!! &lt;3 I CAN’T EVEN!!! *dies of excitement*<br><br><i>”As they moved through the old barn, Adam felt Ronan’s eyes glance off him and away, his disinterest practiced but incomplete. Adam wondered if anyone else noticed.”</i><br><br><i>He admitted, “Some.”<br>“A lot,” Ronan translated, and he was right, because, strangely enough, Ronan knew a great deal about how Adam worked.</i><br><br><i>”Adam and Ronan regarded each other, and then the pit. They looked winsome and brave, trusting of Cabeswater or of each other. They did not look afraid, so Blue was afraid for them.”</i><br><br><b>The conclusion :</b><br><br>Maggie Stiefvater is a poet and a genius!!! I can’t wait to read <b>“The Raven King”</b> and I don’t even dare to say it, but I think I loved this book even more than I loved “The Dream Thieves”! *lol* When it comes to Maggie’s <b>“The Raven Cycle”</b> books there actually seems to be no limit, they only get better and better! &lt;3<br><br><i>“Once I send the professor off, one of you guys can get into the front. Adam? Unless he’s sleeping.”<br>“No,” Adam said. „I’m awake.“</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1513444987i/24691611._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10655796388769971836" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1576271904?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nat" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nat" href="/user/show/23381142-nat">Nat</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23381142-nat?shelf=magical-realism">magical-realism</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1576271904" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6337132616688848740"><i>“Queens and kings<br/>Kings and queens<br/>Blue lily, lily blue<br/>Crowns and birds<br/>Swords and things<br/>Blue lily, lily blue.”</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457801049ra/18407623.gif' width='350' height='210' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/>This review contains <b>*spoilers*</b>.<br/><br/>And just like that, I'm finished.<br/>Now what?<br/>I’ve been reading this series back to back and it made me realize how much I’ve missed the joy (and sleep deprivation) marathoning books gives me.<br/>I already knew how dreadful I would feel once I finished <b>Blue Lily, Lily Blue</b> because I’m in love with these books, but I guess I didn’t prepare myself enough because I CA</span>
  <span id="freeText6337132616688848740" style="display:none"><i>“Queens and kings<br>Kings and queens<br>Blue lily, lily blue<br>Crowns and birds<br>Swords and things<br>Blue lily, lily blue.”</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457801049ra/18407623.gif" width="350" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>This review contains <b>*spoilers*</b>.<br><br>And just like that, I'm finished.<br>Now what?<br>I’ve been reading this series back to back and it made me realize how much I’ve missed the joy (and sleep deprivation) marathoning books gives me.<br>I already knew how dreadful I would feel once I finished <b>Blue Lily, Lily Blue</b> because I’m in love with these books, but I guess I didn’t prepare myself enough because I CAN’T believe I have to wait till April to find out what happens next.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434384ra/876034.gif" width="350" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This series has affected me so much, I love love love the characters and the hilarious banter between all of them. They make me feel at home. And I already miss them. <br>I had no idea going into this world that I would be so addicted to the writing style and the perfectly build up sequences—yet here I am writing this review in the middle of night because I can’t stop thinking about everything that went down in this book.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456431029ra/18234343.gif" width="350" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This book is set shortly after the events of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1573277127?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dream Thieves</a>, Blue and the raven boys continue on with their quest to find Glendower, the Raven King.<br>Maura is still underground in hopes to find Artemus and other mysterious things. <br>And I really missed her in this story, I hadn’t realized what an impact she'd made on me.<br><br><i>“But Maura was not some people. She had begun to dream the future when she was fourteen. She had spoken to her first spirit when she was sixteen. She had used remote viewing to see the other side of the world when she was nineteen. Time and space were bathtubs that Maura splashed in.”</i><br><br>Blue terribly misses her mother, but she remains determined, strong, and compassionate. I loved her in this story.<br><br><i>“After an extraordinary summer full of chasing kings and disappearing mothers, it was hard to really, truly picture herself going to class every day. What would any of this matter in two years? Nobody here would remember her, or vice versa. She would only remember that this was the fall her mother vanished. This was the year of Glendower.”</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442274697ra/16208735.gif" width="340" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Also, Blue and Gansey? I need more of them together.<br><br><i>“Gansey was not sleeping.<br>Because Blue had no cell phone, there was no way for him to break the rules and call her. Instead, he had begun to instead lie in his bed each night, eyes closed, hand resting on his phone, waiting to see if she was going to call him from the Phone/Sewing/Cat Room at her house.<br>Stop it, he told himself. Stop wanting it —<br>His phone buzzed.<br>He put it to his ear.<br>“You’re still not Congress, I see.”<br>He was wide-awake.”</i><br>Their night phone calls made me smile so much. <br><br>And their late night outings even more so.<br><i>“She turned to Gansey.<br>“Blue,” he warned, but his voice was chaotic. This close, his throat was scented with mint and wool sweater and vinyl car seat, and Gansey, just Gansey.<br>She said, “I just want to pretend. I want to pretend that I could.”<br>He breathed out.<br>What was a kiss without a kiss?”</i><br><b>So good and so heartbreaking.</b><br><br><i>“Everything jumbled against everything else in just a few chaotic moments. Fingers in hair, hands cupping necks, mouths dragged on cheeks and chins in dangerous proximity.<br>They stopped, noses mashed against each other in the strange way that closeness required. She could feel his breath in her mouth.<br>“Maybe it wouldn’t hurt if I kiss you,” he whispered. “Maybe it’s only if you kiss me.”</i><br>More of Gansay and Blue together, please. We got lovely little snippets of them together just so we could know how good it can be. But I really really really need more. <br><b>Someone should get kissed in this series</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454768350ra/18012134.gif" width="360" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Speaking of love, there wasn’t as much of Ronan as I would’ve liked but when he did show up—so <i>good</i>. I’m all starry-eyed.<br><br><i>“I want you to whistle or hum or sing, Ronan, and keep track of time,” Gansey said.<br>“You have got to be shitting me,” Ronan replied. “Me.”<br>Gansey peered down the tunnel. “I know you know a lot of songs all the way through, and can do them the same speed and length every time. Because you had to memorize all of those tunes for the Irish music competitions.”</i><br><b>My life will be made when I read more about Ronan’s music competitions. So cute.</b><br><br>And Ronan and Adam’s interactions were so much fun to read, especially when you know that Ronan secretly has feelings for him.<br><br><i>“Later, Adam walked out through the cool, damp night to his small, shitty car. As he sank into the driver’s seat, he found something already sitting on the seat.<br>He retrieved the object and held it up under the feeble interior cab light. It was a small white plastic container. Adam twisted off the lid. Inside was a colorless lotion that smelled of mist and moss. Replacing the lid with a frown, he turned the container over, looking for more identifying features. On the bottom, Ronan’s handwriting labeled it merely: manibus. <u>For your hands.</u>”</i><br><b>He’s so damn sweet and kind and marvelous.</b><br><br><i>“As they moved through the old barn, Adam felt Ronan’s eyes glance off him and away, his disinterest practiced but incomplete. Adam wondered if anyone else noticed. Part of him wished they did and immediately felt bad, because it was vanity, really: See, Adam Parrish is wantable, worthy of a crush, not just by anyone, someone like Ronan, who could want Gansey or anyone else and chose Adam for his hungry eyes.<br>Maybe he was wrong. He could be wrong.”</i><br>So Adam knows? And does he not feel the same?<br>I need <u>answers</u>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448883332ra/17202157.gif" width="350" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><i>“You can be just friends with people, you know,” Orla said. “<b>I think it’s crazy how you’re in love with all those raven boys.</b>”<br>Orla wasn’t wrong, of course. But what she didn’t realize about Blue and her boys was that they were all in love with one another. She was no less obsessed with them than they were with her, or one another, analyzing every conversation and gesture, drawing out every joke into a longer and longer running gag, spending each moment either with one another or thinking about when next they would be with one another. Blue was perfectly aware that it was possible to have a friendship that wasn’t all-encompassing, that wasn’t blinding, deafening, maddening, quickening. It was just that now that she’d had this kind, she didn’t want the other.”</i><br><b>I feel just as close to all the raven boys (especially Ronan)</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457802929ra/18407963.gif" width="350" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Oh, and Robert Parrish visiting Adam was something I definitely wasn’t expecting, but when he showed up at Adam’s door- tears appeared so quickly in my eyes. I still haven’t forgotten that awful night at Adam’s old home.<br><i>“He did not want to get hit.<br>He would do what he needed to do to not get hit.”</i><br><br>Damn, I thought Adam wouldn’t break my heart in this book, but I was so wrong. I was really trying to hold in the tears when he arrived at the courthouse <b>alone</b>. <br><i>“Even if I lose, he thought weakly, he can’t have me back, so it won’t matter. It will only be this hour of humiliation and then it will be over.”</i><br><br>But I was so relieved when the bailiff told the judge that there were some witnesses for the case. I felt like a huge weight had been lifted off of me.<br><br><i>“The door cracked open. Adam didn’t want to look, but he did anyway.<br>In the hall stood Richard Campbell Gansey III in his school uniform and overcoat and scarf and gloves, looking like someone from another world. Behind him was Ronan Lynch, his damn tie knotted right for once and his shirt tucked in.<br>Humiliation and joy warred furiously inside Adam.<br>Gansey strode between the pews as Adam’s father stared at him. He went directly to the bench, straight up to the judge. Now that he stood directly beside Adam, not looking at him, Adam could see that he was a little out of breath. Ronan, behind him, was as well. They had run.<br> <b>For him.</b>”</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388796224ra/7932217.gif" width="350" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>And so much happened towards the end, I’m still trying to wrap my mind it.<br>Especially around the fact that Persephone died. <br><i>“We’ll get her back,” Adam said.<br>But Calla was already crying.<br>Blue, unconcerned with dignity, dragged Persephone out by her armpits. She was light and unresisting.<br>They would pull her back, just as Adam said.<br>Calla sank to her knees and covered her face.<br>“Stop it,” snapped Blue, voice cracking. “Get over here and help.”<br>She took Persephone’s hand. It was as cold as the cave walls.”</i><br>When Calla started crying, I knew something was terribly wrong.<br><b>Calla cries— I cry even harder.</b><br><br><br><i>“Look, I told Calla we were going into the cave. To find Maura.” He corrected, more formally, “Your mother.”<br>“Oh, seriously! Don’t Richard Gansey on me!” Blue snapped, and then, at once, she began to cry.<br>It was against the rules, but Gansey crouched down beside her, one of his knees against her back, one against her knees, and hugged her. She curled against him, hands balled up against his chest. He felt a hot tear slip into the dip of his collarbone. He closed his eyes against the sun through the window, burning hot in his sweater, foot falling asleep, elbow grinding into the metal bed frame, Blue Sargent pressed up against him, and he didn’t move.”</i><br>I love them.<br><br>Their journey into to the cave had me literally on the edge of my seat. I felt like I was holding my breath for those last few pages.<br><br>And when Ronan and Blue saw the lake, I really thought that Maura was gone. This book is seriously destroying me.<br><br><i>“It’s not real,” Ronan told her, voice low. “It’s not real, Blue.”<br>“I saw her,” Blue said, and she heard the sob in her voice. “My mother.”<br>He said, “I know. I saw my father.”<br>“But she was there —”<br>“My father’s dead in the ground. And Adam saw your mother farther on in this godforsaken cave. That lake is a lie.”</i><br><br><i>“For a moment they remained that way, Ronan holding her as tightly as he would hold his brother Matthew, his cheek on her shoulder. Every time she thought she could go on, she saw the face of her mother’s corpse again.<br>Finally, she pulled back, and Ronan stood up. He looked away, but not before she saw the tear he flicked from his chin.<br>“Fuck this,” he said again.”</i><br>I could not handle it when Ronan shed a tear. I love him so much and he doesn’t deserve so much pain. <b>They don’t deserve so much pain.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435254480ra/15322398.gif" width="350" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I love them all so, so much and I could talk about them for hours (thanks Mom for listening).<br>I seriously cannot recommend this book enough. I didn’t so much visit this world as get absorbed. I loved it<br>There wasn't a single moment where I felt bored or lost interest. The story flows so easily.<br>It’s also really painful coming to realize that I won’t know what will happen until April. I can’t let go of the wonderful characters just yet, so I’ll probably read all the really cute scenes over and over.<br><br>Oh, and I <i>finally</i> found the incredible fanart that got me interested in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1571045374?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Raven Boys</a>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457802157i/18407801.jpg" width="200" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Adam Parrish <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457802157i/18407802.jpg" width="200" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457802157i/18407803.jpg" width="200" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Richard Campbell Gansey III<br><a href="http://xla-hainex.tumblr.com/post/136848817636/the-boys-without-noah-though-currently-im" rel="nofollow noopener">Source</a><br><br>I also loved listening to <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4NhKWZpkw1Q" rel="nofollow noopener">this song</a> because my heart was definitely breaking while reading this book.<br><br><i>*Note: I'm an Amazon Affiliate. If you're interested in buying</i> <b>Blue Lily, Lily Blue</b>, <i>just click on the image below to go through my link. I'll make a small commission!*</i><br><a target="_blank" href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00JD36AV8/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B00JD36AV8&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=natalie013-20&amp;linkId=6d8022eddc84da7fff5ef94bdf181bd7" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1482939251i/21564008.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1226994299" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1226994299" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1226994299?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1226994299" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1359501117706985817">I know, I know. Please don't judge me, I'm sick.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470482417ra/19933267.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But it's <b>the sweetest kind of addiction</b>. The one that doesn't let you sleep at nights because your thoughts wander into faraway lands and your heart beats fast for the people you came to love deeply even though they're the products of someone else's brilliant mind and beautiful soul. And I'm not alone, because I'll see you all in therapy, right? <i>Right?</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470425515ra/19928066.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Queens and kings<br/>Kings and Queens<br/>Blue lily, lily blue<br/>Crowns and birds<br/>Swords and things<br/>Blue</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText1359501117706985817" style="display:none">I know, I know. Please don't judge me, I'm sick.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470482417ra/19933267.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But it's <b>the sweetest kind of addiction</b>. The one that doesn't let you sleep at nights because your thoughts wander into faraway lands and your heart beats fast for the people you came to love deeply even though they're the products of someone else's brilliant mind and beautiful soul. And I'm not alone, because I'll see you all in therapy, right? <i>Right?</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470425515ra/19928066.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Queens and kings<br>Kings and Queens<br>Blue lily, lily blue<br>Crowns and birds<br>Swords and things<br>Blue lily, lily blue”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>One</b> missing mother.<br><b>Two</b> arrivals that will endanger everyone in little Henrietta.<br><b>Three</b> sleepers, one to wake up, one to not wake up, and one in between.<br><b>Four</b> boys, a magician, a ghost, a dreamer, a king.<br>And <b>a promise of death</b> as the result of true love's kiss. In most fairytales, true love's kiss is the beginning. In this one, it's the end.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“A lot of promises get broken, Blue.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>As the series progresses, as I fall deeper and deeper in love with the Raven boys and Blue and her crazy family, something cold and malevolent seizes my heart and steals my breath. It's <b>fear</b>. Life-sucking fear. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17378508.Blue_Lily__Lily_Blue__The_Raven_Cycle___3_" title="Blue Lily, Lily Blue (The Raven Cycle, #3) by Maggie Stiefvater" rel="nofollow noopener">Blue Lily, Lily Blue</a>'s atmosphere is heavy and <b>ominous</b> as time passes by, as Gansey's death seems more probable and Blue's love for him intensifies, as more and more people search for the Welsh king and the evil sleeper uses all his mighty force to make someone awaken him. While I dreamed under Henrietta's cloudy sky and heard the whispers of Cabeswater's ancient trees, I begged for a miracle. But I'm not sure I will get one.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I was here. I exist. I’m alive, because I bleed.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>How many powerful emotions are evoked by characters <b>brilliantly flawed</b> and damaged! I finally grew fond of Adam, and sympathized with his loneliness and was happy with the way his relationship with Ronan started to develop. Perhaps they'll find a kindred spirit in each other and share their grief, their anger, and trade them with something more invigorating, something brighter! But while their futute seems full of possibilities, Blue and Gansey follow a path that will result in heartbreak and tears. Probably mine.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Blue,” he warned, but his voice was chaotic. This close, his throat was scented with mint and wool sweater and vinyl car seat, and Gansey, just Gansey.<br>She said, “I just want to pretend. I want to pretend that I could.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392409858ra/8554027.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And it's incurable.<br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17378508.Blue_Lily__Lily_Blue__The_Raven_Cycle___3_" title="Blue Lily, Lily Blue (The Raven Cycle, #3) by Maggie Stiefvater" rel="nofollow noopener">Blue Lily, Lily Blue</a> preludes an intense and all-consuming final book</b>, so I will leave this mundane world for a while and dive into <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17378527.The_Raven_King__The_Raven_Cycle___4_" title="The Raven King (The Raven Cycle, #4) by Maggie Stiefvater" rel="nofollow noopener">The Raven King</a> exhilarated and terrified. Send a prayer my way.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The Raven King, make way for the Raven King.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="1359501117706985817" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">
          

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review1226994299">

<div id="review_2062288941" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2062288941" />
    <a title="emma" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32879029-emma"><img alt="emma" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520568130p2/32879029.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2062288941?book_show_action=true">Aug 18, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="emma" class="user" itemprop="url" name="emma" href="/user/show/32879029-emma">emma</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=owned">owned</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2062288941" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14273481732505112882">HOW DO YOU WRITE A REVIEW OF A BOOK THAT YOU LOVED SO MUCH IT MAKES YOUR HEART WARM AND IT RESTORED YOUR FAITH IN YA AND EVERYTHING IS GOOD IN THE WORLD WHEN YOU THINK ABOUT IT AND FLOWERS BLOOM AND BIRDS FLOAT AROUND YOUR HEAD AND SING OR TWEET OR WHATEVER IT IS THEY DO.<br/><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://emmareadstoomuch.wordpress.com/2017/10/03/blue-lily-lily-blue-review-my-identity-wasnt-stolen-i-promise/'>https://emmareadstoomuch.wordpress.co...</a><br/><br/>No, seriously, please tell me how. Because I straight up read this book a month ago and I GOT NOTHIN'.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505940892ra/23973897.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I suppose I will begin with what I know to be true, and what I know to be true is that</span>
  <span id="freeText14273481732505112882" style="display:none">HOW DO YOU WRITE A REVIEW OF A BOOK THAT YOU LOVED SO MUCH IT MAKES YOUR HEART WARM AND IT RESTORED YOUR FAITH IN YA AND EVERYTHING IS GOOD IN THE WORLD WHEN YOU THINK ABOUT IT AND FLOWERS BLOOM AND BIRDS FLOAT AROUND YOUR HEAD AND SING OR TWEET OR WHATEVER IT IS THEY DO.<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://emmareadstoomuch.wordpress.com/2017/10/03/blue-lily-lily-blue-review-my-identity-wasnt-stolen-i-promise/">https://emmareadstoomuch.wordpress.co...</a><br><br>No, seriously, please tell me how. Because I straight up read this book a month ago and I GOT NOTHIN'.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505940892ra/23973897.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I suppose I will begin with what I know to be true, and what I know to be true is that Richard Gansey III is my husband. I have said this now in three (3) consecutive reviews of each of the three (3) books in this series I have read, and yet it only grows to be more true. Because he only gets <i>better</i>. (What does it say about me that I'm now one hundred percent convinced I just jinxed myself and will hate him by the next book? In other words what is wrong with me. This is a cry for help.)<br><br>I love Gansey. It’s an all-consuming love. It’s above analysis, so I can’t even tell you why I do. But I do. And I’m claiming him. He is THE book boyfriend for me now. (Goodbye, Étienne St. Clair from Anna and the French Kiss. It’s been a good three years, but I’ve grown. I've matured. I’ve moved on. And also, you’re short, and that’s just never been a viable option for me.)<br><br>Me @ every boy of all time:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505941692ra/23973958.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Excluding Gansey (because I could talk about my love for that elegant man-boy for pages I tell ya)...things tend a lot more toward the "eh" end of the spectrum. As in, Ronan is still incredibly blah. Who caaaaaares. We get it. You're edgy. You can stop now. Also, Adam, still sooooooo eh. But I willllll say...a certain relationship begins to blossom and bloom and beautifully pop up from the soil...and that shindig is not eh at all. (Insert the smolder emoji here.)<br><br>But, quelle surprise, nothing is perfect because nothing is ever good or easy, and there is a relationship that is so incredibly eh it's almost like it's too eh for the world eh. Like, they tried to put a picture of this relationship in the dictionary next to the word eh, but they were like one, this is a fictional couple so that's impossible, two, is the word eh even in the dictionary, and three, THIS IS TOO EH EVEN FOR THIS.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501273758ra/23441417.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That's the dictionary people, angrily shouting NEXT, as in "next person proposing an image to be added next to a definition." I bet you didn't consider how much time dealing with those queries takes for the employees of dictionaries.<br><br>ANYWAY. That horribly boring and blah relationship is...sigh...Blue and Gansey. That pairing can die, really. Brutally. That budding duo can get run over by a steamroller and come out all Flat Stanley'd and non-viable on the other side. Also, to clarify, I mean the relationship itself can die. I would never endorse the murder of Gansey.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505941692ra/23973959.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>ANYWAY AGAIN. When did Blue/Gansey <i>happen</i>? One second they're just a pair of pals and the next second they are SMASHING their FACES together PRETENDING they're KISSING. Horrible! Gross! For so many reasons! On so many levels!<br><br>Also, I am not saying this due to any repressed jealousy. That would be insane. And while I may be at a level of insanity that I would call dibs on the hand in marriage of a fictional character, I am not <s>yet</s> at a level of insanity wherein I am jealous of the fictional beaux of that fictional character. That would be, in case anyone is wondering just when this whole thing will officially have gone too far, the moment when help should be contacted.<br><br>But back to the characters. I literally did not even finish that section. God help me. ANYWAY. Blue is pretty cool in this book, because she always is. Noah is still my small spooky son, and I love him and he should’ve been in this book more, but that’s just because he should be in everything. In order for me to attain true happiness I need to reach a point where Noah is popping up even in content not created by Maggie Stiefvater. He’s a goddamn prince and he deserves it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447607005ra/17026670.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Gray Man sticks around for this book, which is a thrill because I love him. (I do not know why this is true, because his literal defining characteristic is that he is gray, but I love him anyway.) AND PLUS, NEW PEOPLE COME. AND GUESS WHAT? THEY'RE ALSO GREAT.<br><br>Piper is a <i>queen.</i> A literal queen, because I am crowning her queen of all villains. This is legitimate and legal in the eyes of the law, because <a href="https://emmareadstoomuch.wordpress.com/2017/08/27/ruler-of-books-tag-i-will-now-only-respond-to-ruler-of-books-or-perhaps-book-queen/" rel="nofollow noopener"> I crowned myself ruler of all books.</a><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505942593ra/23974041.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Piper's husband what's his name is also pretty sick. Which is really surprising, because one, male villains are so boring, and two, Evil Teacher Guy has also been <i>done.</i> Like, within this very series. Two books ago.<br><br>Hahahahaha oh my god. Whoa. I almost forgot about that horrendous bore. What a snoozefest that guy was. The improvement to this series just by this book alone is WILD my friends. WILD.<br><br>But there are even more new people! These include:<br>- a woman who is cool (both the least spoilery AND least interesting way I could possibly put that)<br>- a guy named Jesse who is pretty cute and lovable<br><br>Maggie Stiefvater can really crank out characters I care about. (A feat matched by, guess what, literally no other authors. I am semi-incapable of even fictional love and affection.)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500958936ra/23399834.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The setting remains sick, because it always has been. The magic is even amazing-er than ever. (How does it keep getting better?!)<br><br>This book is just...a more action-packed version of the other two. More of the stuff ya like, less of the same filler sh*t from the first two. You know. Less “Adam is poor and insecure about it, Blue eats yogurt and let’s talk more about the whole amplifier thing, Ronan is angsty, Gansey chews a mint leaf and plays with toys and has a journal and is somehow very rich throughout, Ronan is angsty, Noah is blurry and also, oh yeah, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[dead <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, and of course, Ronan, in case you forgot, is extraordinarily, next-level angsty.”<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505943187ra/23974067.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously, that's a spot on encapsulation of the first two books. I am honestly proud of myself. You could definitely just skip the first two books and cut to what matters based on that paragraph alone. (Please don't do that.)<br><br>I'm quite pleased I didn't give The Raven Boys or The Dream Thieves five stars, because <i>this sh*t is on a whole other level baby.</i> They aren't even in the same REALM OF EXISTENCE. If those two are books this one straight up has to be called something else. We have to make up a new word based on how much better this one is than those garbage monsters. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421678712ra/13403012.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ugh! I am filled with love. And also excitement. And also immense fear and trepidation and regret because oh my god the next one just cannot be as good there is no way it's impossible life is just an endless feast of disappointment with countless courses of sadness casserole, which is also known as just "casserole."<br><br>Um.<br><br>Just realized I'm not going to ever ever read the last book.<br><br>Bottom line: WHATEVER LITERALLY JUST READ THE SERIES FOR THIS BOOK IT IS LIFE-CHANGING AND I KNOW I DID A BAD JOB OF EXPLAINING HOW GREAT IT IS BUT JUST TRUST ME, OK? I'm not used to five star reviews.<br><br>-------------------<br>PRE-REVIEW<br><br>my skin is clear. my bank account is full. my bookshelves aren't messy and my crops survived the winter.<br><br>ok well none of that is true BUT THIS BOOK CHANGED MY STUPID LIFE!!!!!!<br><br>review to come once i resurrect my laptop (even my keyboard died of shock at a five star rating)<br><br>-------------------<br>CURRENTLY-READING UPDATE<br><br>ho<br><br>ly<br><br>shit.<br><br>IS THIS GOING TO BE A FIVE STAR READ?????????</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1575294286?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>
