<div id="review_1577916432" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1577916432" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1577916432?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=ghosts">ghosts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1577916432" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15615593630795163113"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526510418i/25552645._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1453987155?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Raven Boys</a> ★★★★★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1570709343?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Dream Thieves</a> ★★★★★<br/><br/>This book is the physical manifestation of perfection.<br/><br/>This is a once in a lifetime series.<br/><br/>This book's magic fills all my dark places with light. <br/><br/>This series reminded me why I fell in love with reading.<br/><br/>This series is the best thing I've read since <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1454172046?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Harry Potter</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1301719771' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Name of the Wind</a>. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458449110i/18489656._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It's always hard for me to write reviews for books that become my favorites. Hopefully those above five lines will help, or maybe they won't. Either way, no amount</span>
  <span id="freeText15615593630795163113" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526510418i/25552645._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1453987155?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Raven Boys</a> ★★★★★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1570709343?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dream Thieves</a> ★★★★★<br><br>This book is the physical manifestation of perfection.<br><br>This is a once in a lifetime series.<br><br>This book's magic fills all my dark places with light. <br><br>This series reminded me why I fell in love with reading.<br><br>This series is the best thing I've read since <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1454172046?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1301719771" rel="nofollow noopener">The Name of the Wind</a>. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458449110i/18489656._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's always hard for me to write reviews for books that become my favorites. Hopefully those above five lines will help, or maybe they won't. Either way, no amount of words I have can do justice for this masterpiece. You, yourself, should just give this series a chance and see if it puts you under the spell it has placed upon me.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Humans were so circular; they lived the same slow cycles of joy and misery over and over, never learning. Every lesson in the universe had to be taught billions of times, and it never stuck.<br><br>Maybe it was good that the world forgot every lesson, every good and bad memory, every triumph and failure, all of it dying with each generation. Perhaps this cultural amnesia spared them all. Perhaps if they remembered everything, hope would die instead.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>This book really explores a lot of different individualities, and I can't praise Maggie Stiefvater enough. These are the kind of books that YA needs; different stories that are unique, while the characters are different races, different sexualities, with different family dynamics. This book even portrays feminism beautifully, because at this point Blue is my spirit animal. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Everything jumbled against everything else in just a few chaotic moments.<br>Fingers in hair, hands cupping necks, mouths dragged on cheeks and chins in dangerous proximity. <br>They stopped, noses mashed against each other in the strange way that closeness required. <br>She could feel his breath in her mouth.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Blue and Gansey's relationship guts me with every line. Blue's pain resonates with me, and just rips my heart out over and over again. Luckily, I have masochistic tendencies and ask for more. <br><br>I know I've been gushing about diversity and romance, but this book also has a lot of plot to its story. Blue's mom, Maura, is missing and Blue, Mr.Grey, and everyone else, is in a desperate search to get her back. <br><br>Adam and Ronan get more in touch with Cabeswater and start discovering not themselves but each other. <i>*swoons forever*</i><br><br>This book also reintroduces a somewhat new villain, Colin Greenmantle, and his wife Piper. Only this new character will make a much unexpected twist that you won't see coming.<br><br>The gang finds another cave entrance, but finds someone much different than their sleeping Welsh King.<br><br>The anticipation for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17378527-the-raven-king" rel="nofollow noopener"> The Raven King</a> is going to kill me. I keep thinking about and rereading the first chapter of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1453987155?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Raven Boys</a> and I find myself being haunted knowing that I'm going to reread that scene next month in a very different perspective. I don't think there is anything I can do to physically or emotional prepare myself, and mostly my heart, for reading the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17378527-the-raven-king" rel="nofollow noopener">The Raven King</a>. I'm just going to relish in the heartbreak, while trying to remember that I will forever love this series.<br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15615593630795163113" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_924090305" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/924090305" />
    <a title="destini mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia"><img alt="destini mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499903277p2/13742215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/924090305?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destini mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destini mia" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia">destini mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13742215-destini-mia?shelf=the-holy-grail">the-holy-grail</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer924090305" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15915373102881634457"><i>
  <blockquote>“Queens and kings, Kings and queens<br/>Blue lily, lily blue, Crowns and birds <br/>Swords and things, Blue lily, lily blue”</blockquote>
</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459960246i/18679565.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459960246i/18679566.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This series has reduced me to a barely functioning mess, making fan art and listening to fan mixes in my spare time. Which isn't anything wrong, except <b>responsibilities.</b> Responsibilities I have grossly neglected that <i>really</i> need to stop being grossly neglected. <br/><br/>These books <b>just suck you in</b> and take you prisoner. I feel like Maggie Stiefvater is a mad genius or something. The way </span>
  <span id="freeText15915373102881634457" style="display:none"><i>
  <blockquote>“Queens and kings, Kings and queens<br>Blue lily, lily blue, Crowns and birds <br>Swords and things, Blue lily, lily blue”</blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459960246i/18679565.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459960246i/18679566.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This series has reduced me to a barely functioning mess, making fan art and listening to fan mixes in my spare time. Which isn't anything wrong, except <b>responsibilities.</b> Responsibilities I have grossly neglected that <i>really</i> need to stop being grossly neglected. <br><br>These books <b>just suck you in</b> and take you prisoner. I feel like Maggie Stiefvater is a mad genius or something. The way she makes me feel for these characters, <b>it's like a physical ache.</b> Each book makes you feel like a friend, like a familiar, leaving little inside jokes here and there for you to pick up on. It makes you feel like you're a part of their quest, their awfulness and strangeness. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“Everything has gotten so ugly. It wasn’t supposed to be this way.”</blockquote>
</i><br>This is the conclusion of my reread, and I am more convinced than ever that I was <b>so oblivious</b>. What was I do when I <i>thought</i> was I reading this book. I had such a superficial understanding of the workings of this plot and it's only with this reread that I truly understand and am impressed by the intricacies of the tale and complexities of the characters. <br><br>Piper and Colin Greenmantle were awesome additions to the Raven Cycle universe. I feel like my review of this story give off a semi depressing perspective of this series, which isn't a really accurate description because as hopeless and things may be, Maggie Stiefvater finds ways to break the bleak ice. Enter, the Greenmantles.<br><i>
  <blockquote>“Will you marry me?” she asked. <br>He thought about it. “I love myself the most, though. Are you okay always coming in second?”<br>“Samesies,” she replied. <br>
</blockquote>
</i><br>I would love to think I would be the type of girl who'd answer with the same hilariously offhand comment and mean it, but I know my response would be more on the lines of <s>"go sit on a cactus and lose my number"</s> "lol no".<br><br>However, these two were so unapologetically 'evil', and so hilariously... married, that despite how badly they were fucking everything up, I wouldn't have wished it any different. (foreshadowing: I am 100% certain I will regret this statement with the release of <i>The Raven King</i>)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459986675i/18683226.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459986675i/18683227.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>MY SHIPS ARE STRONGER THAN EVER.</b><br><i>
  <blockquote>“And then we never speak of it again,” Gansey said, mocking himself softly, and Blue was so glad of it, because she had played the words from that night over and over in her mind and wanted to know he had, too.</blockquote>
</i><br>The impossibility of them together makes it so savagely sweet. Every moment they spend together leaves you heady, waiting on the next moment before the first one has even finished. You know these stolen moments are not enough. You <i>know</i> Gansey is living on borrowed time and even that will give out soon enough.<br><i>
  <blockquote>Ronan and Adam kept vanishing places together... </blockquote>
</i><br>Ronan and Adam kept vanishing places together...<br><b>Ronan and Adam kept vanishing places together...</b><br><b>
  <i>Ronan and Adam kept vanishing places together...</i>
</b><br><u>RONAN AND ADAM KEPT VANISHING PLACES TOGETHER</u>...<br><br>*screaming internally*<br>*screaming externally*<br>*screaming eternally*<br><i>
  <blockquote>It was time to find Glendower. They all knew it.</blockquote>
</i><br>My heart is so full. <b>Full of Welsh kings, and <u>late night phone calls</u>, secret meetings, stolen touches, lost mothers, whispering trees, and the unavoidable awareness that <i>each moment brings us closer to the end</i></b>. When Glendower is found. When Gansey is dead. When everything will have to go back to normal, <u>except we've all forgotten what normal even is</u>. <br><i>
  <blockquote> Soon it would be behind him. Soon this school year, too would be behind him. Soon they would find Glendower, soon they would all be kings. Soon, soon.</blockquote>
</i><br><b>OLD REVIEW</b>--&gt;<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>I'm still awestruck by how <i><b>incredible</b></i> that was. I had <b><u>ridiculously</u></b> high expectations for this book . . . so high that I pretty much set <i>Blue Lily, Lily Blue</i> up for failure. And yet, Maggie Stiefvater still managed to astound me. <br><blockquote><b>There is danger in dreaming. But there is even more danger in waking up.<br><br>Blue Sargent has found things. For the first time in her life, she has friends she can trust, a group to which she can belong. The Raven Boys have taken her in as one of their own. Their problems have become hers, and her problems have become theirs.<br><br>The trick with found things though, is how easily they can be lost.<br><br>Friends can betray.<br>Mothers can disappear.<br>Visions can mislead.<br>Certainties can unravel.</b></blockquote>
<br><br>I am such a huge fan of this series. I feel like I could reread these books for years and still find something new to be fascinated by. The story and characters are so complex that you can't help but be sucked right in. It's been some <i>loooooonnnngggg</i>, torturous months since I finished <i>The Dream Thieves</i> and I was able to sink into the story as if I had started this series yesterday. <br><i><blockquote>“It is not the outside of people that bothers me, but the inside.” </blockquote></i><br><br><i>Blue Lily, Lily Blue</i> and the rest of the <i>Raven Cycle</i> series has a really <b>unique</b> story. Yes, it deals with the paranormal . . . witches, clairvoyance, etc. but Stiefvater puts an extraordinary twist on a simple concept, that you can't compare it to anything else. <br><br>The characters are so <i><b>real</b></i> and so <b><i>layered</i></b> that you immediately form and attachment to them. They're constantly evolving and growing and I'm constantly learning something new about them and trying to catch up. They take a life of their own and I've become such a hardcore fangirl. <br><i><blockquote> What a lie unknowable was. The only person who didn't know Adam was himself.</blockquote></i><br>I love how, although there is romance in this series, it doesn't take up its entire focus. I usually like my books heavy on the lovey-dovey stuff but this story is strong enough to stand on its own. Don't get me wrong, it's always welcome *nudges author with not so subtle hint* but I'm just as entranced by the story. <br><br><br>Maggie Stiefvater has a gift for storytelling and the writing in <i>Blue Lily, Lily Blue</i> was beyond amazing. She creates such witty and organic characters that she even has me liking the villains. If I had a physical copy, half it's weight would be due to all the highlighter ink that would've been used. That's how much I love her writing. Instead, I have an endless scroll of quotes on my iPad. <br><br><b>So, just some things . . . </b><br><br>1. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Ronan x Adam –&gt; I will not rest until this happens.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>2. Oh, Noah . . . we see the least of him out of all the Raven Boys but he holds a special place in my heart. He's so fragile that I just want to take him in my arms and never let anything happen to him again. <br><br><br>3. Adam . . . surprised me. He really grew as a character and I felt like a proud mom watching him mature *sniffles a little* <br><br>4. Ever since <i>The Dream Thieves</i>, Ronan has had my heart and will forever have my heart. He can be an asshole, but I just take that as a sign that he cares. <br><br>5. Gansey x Blue –&gt; it seems so hopeless and inevitable . . . I don't know whether to cheer for that or rage over the fact that if they ever act on their feelings it'll all end in disaster. Raven Cycle without Gansey = death of my heart . . . Raven Cycle without Blue x Gansey = death of my heart . . . I have a problem here. <br><br>I could literally dedicate a whole review on why they belong together. Happy . . . in love . . . <b>ALIVE.</b><br><i><blockquote>“And then we never speak of it again,” Gansey said, mocking himself softly, and Blue was so glad of it, because she had played the words from that night over and over in her mind and wanted to know he had, too.</blockquote></i><br><br><b>All in all, book 3 is just another reason why I love this series so much and why it will always be my favorite. </b><br><i><blockquote> . . . what she didn't realize about Blue and her boys was that they were all in love with one another. She was no less obsessed with them than they were with her, or one another, analyzing every conversation and gesture, drawing out every joke into a longer and longer running gag, spending each moment either with one another or thinking about when next they would be with one another.</blockquote></i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>.::MY REVIEW FOR::.</b><br>⚬ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1596781061?comment=149957545#comment_form" rel="nofollow noopener">The Raven Boys</a> (book 1)<br>⚬ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/923246864?type=review#rating_72160451" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dream Thieves</a> (book 2)<br>⚬ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1082002600?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Raven King</a> (book 4)<br><br><b>.::ALSO, FOR ANYONE INTERESTED::.</b><br>⚬ This is the most Bluesy song I have ever heard: <a href="https://www.google.com/url?sa=t&amp;rct=j&amp;q=&amp;esrc=s&amp;source=web&amp;cd=1&amp;cad=rja&amp;uact=8&amp;ved=0ahUKEwi70tC6sfbLAhWBXh4KHSs9DiUQyCkIIDAA&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3D2oI-BsWbIg4&amp;usg=AFQjCNE1Y9vz_kBsibriTJlhjZATIBRUdA" rel="nofollow noopener">Drive</a><br><br><i>Your laugh echoes down the hallway<br>Carves into my hollow chest, spreads over the emptiness<br>It's bliss<br>It's so simple but we can't stay<br>Over analyze again, would it really kill you if we kissed?<br><br>All we do is drive<br>All we do is think about the feelings that we hide<br>All we do is sit in silence waiting for a sign<br>Sick and full of pride<br>All we do is drive</i><br><br>⚬ This is the most Pynch song I have ever heard: <a href="https://www.google.com/url?sa=t&amp;rct=j&amp;q=&amp;esrc=s&amp;source=web&amp;cd=1&amp;cad=rja&amp;uact=8&amp;sqi=2&amp;ved=0ahUKEwjhyrbbsfbLAhXJuB4KHTFKCiUQyCkIHzAA&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3DPVjiKRfKpPI&amp;usg=AFQjCNHfz1Mn4L4DSEyLl9IGmsqJ1pLdkg&amp;bvm=bv.118443451,d.dmo" rel="nofollow noopener">Take Me To Church</a><br><br><i>No masters or kings when the ritual begins<br>There is no sweeter innocence than our gentle sin<br>In the madness and soil of that sad earthly scene<br>Only then I am human<br>Only then I am clean<br>Amen. //<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vpb3iQoSi3dk8Ulc6mrlxGG8kMEBUDkzh0l1TvZjxYZek6ymJ8gNoRUHb3f4cOHBg4jIhkjKPjhSBo+I+gBTuQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pK3O23B8w/Zn/azjfzgIkbP2/LiawhRA/1WUcLb4TY1EqJX0XaZFIBYLishtIgyUUcKk/9NYE0sqGm62upvbsg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

Maggie Stiefvater lives in the middle of nowhere, Virginia with her charmingly straight-laced husband, two kids, two neurotic dogs, and a 1973 Camaro named Loki.<br /><br /></span>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/24170141-blue-lily-lily-blue">Quotes from Blue Lily, Lily Blue</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;You can be just friends with people, you know," Orla said. "I think it's crazy how you're in love with all those raven boys."<br /><br />Orla wasn't wrong, of course. But what she didn't realize about Blue and her boys was that they were all in love with one another. She was no less obsessed with them than they were with her, or one another, analyzing every conversation and gesture, drawing out every joke into a longer and longer running gag, spending each moment either with one another or thinking about when next they would be with one another. Blue was perfectly aware that it was possible to have a friendship that wasn't all-encompassing, that wasn't blinding, deafening, maddening, quickening. It was just that now that she'd had this kind, she didn't want the other.&rdquo;</span>
